<h5 class="kt-adv-heading79881_458476-0f wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-theme-palette-5-background-color has-background" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading79881_458476-0f">Meet the author</h5>



<h2 class="kt-adv-heading79881_5399f8-a3 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading79881_5399f8-a3">Welcome to The Bite!</h2>



<p class="has-text-align-center">Hi! I&#8217;m Jackie, the face behind <br>The Bite with Jackie. Here, I&#8217;ll be sharing my favorite recipes with you in, many of which are inspired by the Arab heritage and stem from some of my fondest memories of home. From the smell of warm spices, to the sounds of stews bubbling away and filling the house with a comforting scent. I hope you are inspired to get in the kitchen and that these recipes give you a taste of home!</p>
